I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Feature Request: Support `YEAR` placeholder in `hack/boilerplate.go.txt`
### What do you want to happen?

The scaffolded `hack/boilerplate.go.txt` currently contains a hard-coded copyright year (e.g. `Copyright 2026 The Kubernetes authors.`). Over time this becomes stale. Both [gengo](https://github.com/kubernetes/gengo/blob/5ee0d033ba5bcb073f0e69c32057520b82d75ccb/v2/execute.go#L59)[^1] and [controller-gen](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-tools/pull/544)[^2] already support a `YEAR` placeholder that is substituted with the current year at code-generation time.

### Proposed change

1. **Scaffold `YEAR` instead of a resolved year.** `kubebuilder init` writes `Copyright YEAR The Kubernetes authors.` into `hack/boilerplate.go.txt` rather than the current year.

2. **Substitute `YEAR` when scaffolding files.** When kubebuilder reads `boilerplate.go.txt` from disk before scaffolding new files (e.g. `kubebuilder create api`), it replaces `YEAR` with the current year — matching gengo's behavior — so generated Go files always get the correct year in their header.

3. **Pass `year=$(YEAR)` to `controller-gen` in the generated `Makefile`.** The `generate` target becomes:
   ```makefile
   YEAR ?= $(shell date +%Y)
   ...
   "$(CONTROLLER_GEN)" object:headerFile="hack/boilerplate.go.txt",year=$(YEAR) paths="./..."
   ```
   This uses the `year=` option introduced in [controller-tools#544](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-tools/pull/544) so `make generate` also resolves the placeholder in DeepCopy file headers.

### Why this is useful

- Copyright years in scaffolded files are always current without any manual edits.
- Consistent with the conventions already established in gengo and controller-gen.
- The `YEAR` variable in the Makefile can be overridden by the user (`make generate YEAR=2024`) for edge cases.

---


[^1]: https://github.com/kubernetes/gengo/blob/5ee0d033ba5bcb073f0e69c32057520b82d75ccb/v2/execute.go#L59
[^2]: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-tools/pull/544

### Extra Labels

     5	you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
     6	You may obtain a copy of the License at
     7	
     8	    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
     9	
    10	Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
    11	distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
    12	WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
    13	See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
    14	limitations under the License.
    15	*/
    16	
    17	package hack
    18	
    19	import (
    20	        "fmt"
    21	        "path/filepath"
    22	        "time"
    23	
    24	        "sigs.k8s.io/kubebuilder/v4/pkg/machinery"
    25	)
    26	
    27	// DefaultBoilerplatePath is the default path to the boilerplate file
    28	var DefaultBoilerplatePath = filepath.Join("hack", "boilerplate.go.txt")
    29	
    30	var _ machinery.Template = &Boilerplate{}
    31	
    32	// Boilerplate scaffolds a file that defines the common header for the rest of the files
    33	type Boilerplate struct {
    34	        machinery.TemplateMixin
    35	        machinery.BoilerplateMixin
    36	
    37	        // License is the License type to write
    38	        License string
    39	
    40	        // Licenses maps License types to their actual string
    41	        Licenses map[string]string
    42	
    43	        // Owner is the copyright owner - e.g. "The Kubernetes Authors"
    44	        Owner string
    45	
    46	        // Year is the copyright year
    47	        Year string
    48	}
    49	
    50	// Validate implements file.RequiresValidation
    51	func (f *Boilerplate) Validate() error {
    52	        if f.License != "" {
    53	                if _, foundKnown := knownLicenses[f.License]; !foundKnown {
    54	                        if _, found := f.Licenses[f.License]; !found {
    55	                                return fmt.Errorf("unknown specified license %s", f.License)
    56	                        }
    57	                }
    58	        }
    59	        return nil
    60	}
    61	
    62	// SetTemplateDefaults implements machinery.Template
    63	func (f *Boilerplate) SetTemplateDefaults() error {
    64	        if f.Path == "" {
    65	                f.Path = DefaultBoilerplatePath
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        if f.License == "" {
    69	                f.License = "apache2"
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        if f.Licenses == nil {
    73	                f.Licenses = make(map[string]string, len(knownLicenses))
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        for key, value := range knownLicenses {
    77	                if _, hasLicense := f.Licenses[key]; !hasLicense {
    78	                        f.Licenses[key] = value
    79	                }
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        if f.Year == "" {
    83	                f.Year = fmt.Sprintf("%v", time.Now().Year())
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        // Boilerplate given
    87	        if len(f.Boilerplate) > 0 {
    88	                f.TemplateBody = f.Boilerplate
    89	                return nil
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        f.TemplateBody = boilerplateTemplate
    93	
    94	        return nil
    95	}
    96	
    97	const boilerplateTemplate = `/*
    98	{{ if .Owner -}}
    99	Copyright {{ .Year }} {{ .Owner }}.
   100	{{- else -}}
   101	Copyright {{ .Year }}.
   102	{{- end }}
   103	{{ index .Licenses .License }}*/`
   104	
   105	var knownLicenses = map[string]string{
   106	        "apache2":   apache2,
   107	        "copyright": "",
   108	}
   109	
   110	const apache2 = `
   111	Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
   112	you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
   113	You may obtain a copy of the License at
   114	
   115	    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
   116	
   117	Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
   118	distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
   119	WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
   120	See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
   121	limitations under the License.
   122	`
   123

    36	var _ plugins.Scaffolder = &apiScaffolder{}
    37	
    38	// apiScaffolder contains configuration for generating scaffolding for Go type
    39	// representing the API and controller that implements the behavior for the API.
    40	type apiScaffolder struct {
    41	        config   config.Config
    42	        resource resource.Resource
    43	
    44	        // fs is the filesystem that will be used by the scaffolder
    45	        fs machinery.Filesystem
    46	
    47	        // force indicates whether to scaffold controller files even if it exists or not
    48	        force bool
    49	}
    50	
    51	// NewAPIScaffolder returns a new Scaffolder for API/controller creation operations
    52	func NewAPIScaffolder(cfg config.Config, res resource.Resource, force bool) plugins.Scaffolder {
    53	        return &apiScaffolder{
    54	                config:   cfg,
    55	                resource: res,
    56	                force:    force,
    57	        }
    58	}
    59	
    60	// InjectFS implements cmdutil.Scaffolder
    61	func (s *apiScaffolder) InjectFS(fs machinery.Filesystem) {
    62	        s.fs = fs
    63	}
    64	
    65	// Scaffold implements cmdutil.Scaffolder
    66	func (s *apiScaffolder) Scaffold() error {
    67	        log.Info("Writing scaffold for you to edit...")
    68	
    69	        // Load the boilerplate
    70	        boilerplate, err := afero.ReadFile(s.fs.FS, hack.DefaultBoilerplatePath)
    71	        if err != nil {
    72	                if errors.Is(err, afero.ErrFileNotFound) {
    73	                        log.Warn("unable to find boilerplate file. "+
    74	                                "This file is used to generate the license header in the project.\n"+
    75	                                "Note that controller-gen will also use this. Ensure that you "+
    76	                                "add the license file or configure your project accordingly",
    77	                                "file_path", hack.DefaultBoilerplatePath, "error", err)
    78	                        boilerplate = []byte("")
    79	                } else {
    80	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffolding API/controller: failed to load boilerplate: %w", err)
    81	                }
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        // Initialize the machinery.Scaffold that will write the files to disk
    85	        scaffold := machinery.NewScaffold(s.fs,
    86	                machinery.WithConfig(s.config),
    87	                machinery.WithBoilerplate(string(boilerplate)),
    88	                machinery.WithResource(&s.resource),
    89	        )
    90	
    91	        // Keep track of these values before the update
    92	        doAPI := s.resource.HasAPI()
    93	        doController := s.resource.HasController()
    94	
    95	        if err := s.config.UpdateResource(s.resource); err != nil {
    96	                return fmt.Errorf("error updating resource: %w", err)
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        if doAPI {
   100	                if err := scaffold.Execute(
   101	                        &api.Types{Force: s.force},
   102	                        &api.Group{},
   103	                ); err != nil {
   104	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffolding APIs: %w", err)
   105	                }
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        if doController {
   109	                if err := scaffold.Execute(
   110	                        &controllers.SuiteTest{Force: s.force},
   111	                        &controllers.Controller{ControllerRuntimeVersion: ControllerRuntimeVersion, Force: s.force},
   112	                        &controllers.ControllerTest{Force: s.force, DoAPI: doAPI},
   113	                ); err != nil {
   114	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffolding controller: %w", err)
   115	                }
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if err := scaffold.Execute(
   119	                &cmd.MainUpdater{WireResource: doAPI, WireController: doController},
   120	        ); err != nil {
   121	                return fmt.Errorf("error updating cmd/main.go: %w", err)
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        return nil
   125	}

    71	// Scaffold implements cmdutil.Scaffolder
    72	func (s *webhookScaffolder) Scaffold() error {
    73	        log.Info("Writing scaffold for you to edit...")
    74	
    75	        // Load the boilerplate
    76	        boilerplate, err := afero.ReadFile(s.fs.FS, hack.DefaultBoilerplatePath)
    77	        if err != nil {
    78	                if errors.Is(err, afero.ErrFileNotFound) {
    79	                        log.Warn("unable to find boilerplate file. "+
    80	                                "This file is used to generate the license header in the project..\n"+
    81	                                "Note that controller-gen will also use this. Ensure that you "+
    82	                                "add the license file or configure your project accordingly",
    83	                                "file_path", hack.DefaultBoilerplatePath, "error", err)
    84	                        boilerplate = []byte("")
    85	                } else {
    86	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffolding webhook: failed to load boilerplate: %w", err)
    87	                }
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        // Initialize the machinery.Scaffold that will write the files to disk
    91	        scaffold := machinery.NewScaffold(s.fs,
    92	                machinery.WithConfig(s.config),
    93	                machinery.WithBoilerplate(string(boilerplate)),
    94	                machinery.WithResource(&s.resource),
    95	        )
    96	
    97	        // Keep track of these values before the update
    98	        doDefaulting := s.resource.HasDefaultingWebhook()
    99	        doValidation := s.resource.HasValidationWebhook()
   100	        doConversion := s.resource.HasConversionWebhook()
   101	
   102	        if err = s.config.UpdateResource(s.resource); err != nil {
   103	                return fmt.Errorf("error updating resource: %w", err)
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        // Check if webhook files exist
   107	        webhookFilePath := s.getWebhookFilePath()
   108	        webhookFileExists := false
   109	        if _, statErr := s.fs.FS.Stat(webhookFilePath); statErr == nil {
   110	                webhookFileExists = true
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        webhookTestFilePath := s.getWebhookTestFilePath()
   114	        webhookTestFileExists := false
   115	        if _, statErr := s.fs.FS.Stat(webhookTestFilePath); statErr == nil {
   116	                webhookTestFileExists = true
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        // Scaffold or update webhook file (for all webhook types)
   120	        // Note: Conversion webhooks also need a webhook.go file with minimal setup (.For(&Type{}).Complete())
   121	        // This is how controller-runtime discovers Hub/Convertible interfaces
   122	        if doDefaulting || doValidation || doConversion {
   123	                if err = s.scaffoldWebhookFile(scaffold, webhookFileExists); err != nil {
   124	                        return err
   125	                }
   126	
   127	                // Update main.go to wire webhook setup function (for all webhook types)
   128	                if err = scaffold.Execute(
   129	                        &cmd.MainUpdater{WireWebhook: true, IsLegacyPath: s.isLegacy},
   130	                ); err != nil {
   131	                        return fmt.Errorf("error updating main.go: %w", err)
   132	                }
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        // Scaffold or update webhook test file (for all webhook types)
   136	        if err = s.scaffoldWebhookTestFile(scaffold, webhookTestFileExists); err != nil {
   137	                return err
   138	        }
   139	
   140	        // Update e2e tests
   141	        // WireWebhook controls webhook service readiness checks (for defaulting/validation)
   142	        // But conversion webhooks still need CA injection tests (handled inside updater)
   143	        if err = scaffold.Execute(
   144	                &e2e.WebhookTestUpdater{WireWebhook: doDefaulting || doValidation},
   145	        ); err != nil {
   146	                return fmt.Errorf("error updating e2e tests: %w", err)
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        if doConversion {
   150	                // Update the types file to add storage version marker
   151	                if err = scaffold.Execute(&api.TypesUpdater{}); err != nil {
   152	                        return fmt.Errorf("error updating types file with storage version marker: %w", err)
   153	                }
   154	
   155	                if err = scaffold.Execute(&api.Hub{Force: s.force}); err != nil {
   156	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffold resource with hub: %w", err)
   157	                }
   158	
   159	                for _, spoke := range s.resource.Webhooks.Spoke {
   160	                        log.Info("Scaffolding for spoke version", "version", spoke)
   161	                        if err = scaffold.Execute(&api.Spoke{Force: s.force, SpokeVersion: spoke}); err != nil {
   162	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to scaffold spoke %s: %w", spoke, err)
   163	                        }
   164	                }
   165	
   166	                log.Info(`Webhook server has been set up for you.
   167	You need to implement the conversion.Hub and conversion.Convertible interfaces for your CRD types.`)
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        // Scaffold webhook suite test for all webhook types
   171	        // Note: Conversion webhooks also need the suite to register with envtest
   172	        if doDefaulting || doValidation || doConversion {
   173	                if err = scaffold.Execute(&webhooks.WebhookSuite{IsLegacyPath: s.isLegacy}); err != nil {
   174	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffold webhook suite: %w", err)
   175	                }
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        // TODO: remove for go/v5
   179	        if !s.isLegacy {
   180	                if hasInternalController, err := pluginutil.HasFileContentWith("Dockerfile", "internal/controller"); err != nil {
   181	                        log.Error("failed to read Dockerfile to check if webhook(s) will be properly copied", "error", err)
   182	                } else if hasInternalController {
   183	                        log.Warn("Dockerfile is copying internal/controller; to allow copying webhooks, " +
   184	                                "it will be edited, and `internal/controller` will be replaced by `internal/`")
   185	
   186	                        if err = pluginutil.ReplaceInFile("Dockerfile", "internal/controller", "internal/"); err != nil {
   187	                                log.Error("failed to replace \"internal/controller\" with \"internal/\" in the Dockerfile", "error", err)
   188	                        }
   189	                }
   190	        }
   191	        return nil
   192	}
   193	
   194	// getWebhookFilePath returns the path to the webhook file
   195	func (s *webhookScaffolder) getWebhookFilePath() string {
   196	        baseDir := "api"
   197	        if !s.isLegacy {
   198	                baseDir = "internal/webhook"
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        var path string
   202	        if s.config.IsMultiGroup() && s.resource.Group != "" {
   203	                path = fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s/%s/%s_webhook.go",
   204	                        baseDir, s.resource.Group, s.resource.Version, strings.ToLower(s.resource.Kind))
   205	        } else {
   206	                path = fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s/%s_webhook.go",
   207	                        baseDir, s.resource.Version, strings.ToLower(s.resource.Kind))
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        return path
   211	}
   212	
   213	// getWebhookTestFilePath returns the path to the webhook test file
   214	func (s *webhookScaffolder) getWebhookTestFilePath() string {
   215	        baseDir := "api"
   216	        if !s.isLegacy {
   217	                baseDir = "internal/webhook"
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        var path string
   221	        if s.config.IsMultiGroup() && s.resource.Group != "" {
   222	                path = fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s/%s/%s_webhook_test.go",
   223	                        baseDir, s.resource.Group, s.resource.Version, strings.ToLower(s.resource.Kind))
   224	        } else {
   225	                path = fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s/%s_webhook_test.go",
   226	                        baseDir, s.resource.Version, strings.ToLower(s.resource.Kind))
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        return path
   230	}

   232	// scaffoldWebhookFile creates or updates the webhook implementation file
   233	func (s *webhookScaffolder) scaffoldWebhookFile(scaffold *machinery.Scaffold, fileExists bool) error {
   234	        if !fileExists || s.force {
   235	                if err := scaffold.Execute(
   236	                        &webhooks.Webhook{Force: s.force, IsLegacyPath: s.isLegacy},
   237	                ); err != nil {
   238	                        return fmt.Errorf("error creating webhook: %w", err)
   239	                }
   240	        } else if fileExists && !s.force && !s.isLegacy {
   241	                log.Info("Adding new webhook type to existing file")
   242	                if err := scaffold.Execute(
   243	                        &webhooks.WebhookUpdater{},
   244	                ); err != nil {
   245	                        return fmt.Errorf("error updating webhook: %w", err)
   246	                }
   247	        }
   248	        return nil
   249	}
   250	
   251	// scaffoldWebhookTestFile creates or updates the webhook test file
   252	func (s *webhookScaffolder) scaffoldWebhookTestFile(scaffold *machinery.Scaffold, fileExists bool) error {
   253	        if !fileExists || s.force {
   254	                if err := scaffold.Execute(
   255	                        &webhooks.WebhookTest{Force: s.force, IsLegacyPath: s.isLegacy},
   256	                ); err != nil {
   257	                        return fmt.Errorf("error creating webhook test: %w", err)
   258	                }
   259	        } else if fileExists && !s.force && !s.isLegacy {
   260	                if err := scaffold.Execute(
   261	                        &webhooks.WebhookTestUpdater{},
   262	                ); err != nil {
   263	                        return fmt.Errorf("error updating webhook test: %w", err)
   264	                }
   265	        }
   266	        return nil

    96	// Scaffold implements cmdutil.Scaffolder
    97	func (s *initScaffolder) Scaffold() error {
    98	        log.Info("Writing scaffold for you to edit...")
    99	
   100	        // Initialize the machinery.Scaffold that will write the boilerplate file to disk
   101	        // The boilerplate file needs to be scaffolded as a separate step as it is going to
   102	        // be used by the rest of the files, even those scaffolded in this command call.
   103	        scaffold := machinery.NewScaffold(s.fs,
   104	                machinery.WithConfig(s.config),
   105	        )
   106	
   107	        if s.license != "none" {
   108	                bpFile := &hack.Boilerplate{
   109	                        License: s.license,
   110	                        Owner:   s.owner,
   111	                }
   112	                bpFile.Path = s.boilerplatePath
   113	                if err := scaffold.Execute(bpFile); err != nil {
   114	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to execute boilerplate: %w", err)
   115	                }
   116	
   117	                boilerplate, err := afero.ReadFile(s.fs.FS, s.boilerplatePath)
   118	                if err != nil {
   119	                        if errors.Is(err, afero.ErrFileNotFound) {
   120	                                log.Warn("unable to find boilerplate file. "+
   121	                                        "This file is used to generate the license header in the project.\n"+
   122	                                        "Note that controller-gen will also use this. Ensure that you "+
   123	                                        "add the license file or configure your project accordingly",
   124	                                        "file_path", s.boilerplatePath,
   125	                                        "error", err)
   126	                                boilerplate = []byte("")
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to load boilerplate: %w", err)
   129	                        }
   130	                }
   131	                // Initialize the machinery.Scaffold that will write the files to disk
   132	                scaffold = machinery.NewScaffold(s.fs,
   133	                        machinery.WithConfig(s.config),
   134	                        machinery.WithBoilerplate(string(boilerplate)),
   135	                )
   136	        } else {
   137	                s.boilerplatePath = ""
   138	                // Initialize the machinery.Scaffold without boilerplate
   139	                scaffold = machinery.NewScaffold(s.fs,
   140	                        machinery.WithConfig(s.config),
   141	                )
   142	        }
   143	
   144	        // If the KustomizeV2 was used to do the scaffold then
   145	        // we need to ensure that we use its supported Kustomize Version
   146	        // in order to support it
   147	        kustomizev2 := kustomizecommonv2.Plugin{}
   148	        gov4 := "go.kubebuilder.io/v4"
   149	        pluginKeyForKustomizeV2 := plugin.KeyFor(kustomizev2)
   150	
   151	        for _, pluginKey := range s.config.GetPluginChain() {
   152	                if pluginKey == pluginKeyForKustomizeV2 || pluginKey == gov4 {
   153	                        kustomizeVersion = kustomizecommonv2.KustomizeVersion
   154	                        break
   155	                }
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        err := scaffold.Execute(
   159	                &cmd.Main{
   160	                        ControllerRuntimeVersion: ControllerRuntimeVersion,
   161	                },
   162	                &templates.GoMod{
   163	                        ControllerRuntimeVersion: ControllerRuntimeVersion,
   164	                },
   165	                &templates.GitIgnore{},
   166	                &templates.Makefile{
   167	                        Image:                    imageName,
   168	                        BoilerplatePath:          s.boilerplatePath,
   169	                        ControllerToolsVersion:   ControllerToolsVersion,
   170	                        KustomizeVersion:         kustomizeVersion,
   171	                        GolangciLintVersion:      GolangciLintVersion,
   172	                        ControllerRuntimeVersion: ControllerRuntimeVersion,
   173	                        EnvtestVersion:           getControllerRuntimeReleaseBranch(),
   174	                },
   175	                &templates.Dockerfile{},
   176	                &templates.DockerIgnore{},

    23	var _ machinery.Template = &Makefile{}
    24	
    25	// Makefile scaffolds a file that defines project management CLI commands
    26	type Makefile struct {
    27	        machinery.TemplateMixin
    28	        machinery.ProjectNameMixin
    29	
    30	        // Image is controller manager image name
    31	        Image string
    32	        // BoilerplatePath is the path to the boilerplate file
    33	        BoilerplatePath string
    34	        // Controller tools version to use in the project
    35	        ControllerToolsVersion string
    36	        // Kustomize version to use in the project
    37	        KustomizeVersion string
    38	        // golangci-lint version to use in the project
    39	        GolangciLintVersion string
    40	        // ControllerRuntimeVersion version to be used to download the envtest setup script
    41	        ControllerRuntimeVersion string
    42	        // EnvtestVersion store the name of the verions to be used to install setup-envtest
    43	        EnvtestVersion string
    44	}
    45	
    46	// SetTemplateDefaults implements machinery.Template
    47	func (f *Makefile) SetTemplateDefaults() error {
    48	        if f.Path == "" {
    49	                f.Path = "Makefile"
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        f.TemplateBody = makefileTemplate
    53	
    54	        f.IfExistsAction = machinery.Error
    55	
    56	        if f.Image == "" {
    57	                f.Image = "controller:latest"
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        // TODO: Current workaround for setup-envtest compatibility
    61	        // Due to past instances where controller-runtime maintainers released
    62	        // versions without corresponding branches, directly relying on branches
    63	        // poses a risk of breaking the Kubebuilder chain. Such practices may
    64	        // change over time, potentially leading to compatibility issues. This
    65	        // approach, although not ideal, remains the best solution for ensuring
    66	        // compatibility with controller-runtime releases as of now. For more
    67	        // details on the quest for a more robust solution, refer to the issue
    68	        // raised in the controller-runtime repository: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-runtime/issues/2744
    69	        if f.EnvtestVersion == "" {
    70	                f.EnvtestVersion = "latest"
    71	        }
    72	        return nil
    73	}

   104	# target descriptions by '##'. The awk command is responsible for reading the
   105	# entire set of makefiles included in this invocation, looking for lines of the

   107	# if there's a line with ##@ something, that gets pretty-printed as a category.

cat > /tmp/repro_year.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
current_year=$(date +%Y)

# init scaffolded boilerplate should keep the YEAR placeholder, not resolve to the current year.
grep -q 'Copyright {{ .Year }} {{ .Owner }}\.' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/hack/boilerplate.go && {
  echo 'FAIL: boilerplate template still renders resolved .Year instead of YEAR placeholder'
  exit 1
}
grep -q 'Copyright YEAR {{ .Owner }}\.' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/hack/boilerplate.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: boilerplate template does not scaffold YEAR placeholder'
  exit 1
}

# generated Makefile should define overridable YEAR and pass it to controller-gen.
grep -q '^\s*YEAR ?= \$(shell date +%Y)' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/makefile.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: Makefile template does not define YEAR ?= $(shell date +%Y)'
  exit 1
}
grep -q 'object:headerFile={{printf "%q" .BoilerplatePath}},year=\$(YEAR)' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/makefile.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: Makefile template does not pass year=$(YEAR) to controller-gen with headerFile'
  exit 1
}

# boilerplate read from disk for subsequent scaffolding should replace YEAR with current year.
for file in \
  pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/api.go \
  pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/webhook.go \
  pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/init.go \
  pkg/plugins/golang/deploy-image/v1alpha1/scaffolds/api.go; do
  grep -q 'ReplaceAll(string(boilerplate), "YEAR", fmt.Sprintf("%d", time.Now().Year()))' "$file" || {
    echo "FAIL: $file does not replace YEAR in boilerplate before injecting it"
    exit 1
  }
done

echo 'PASS: YEAR placeholder support appears implemented'
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_year.sh

    40	var _ plugins.Scaffolder = &apiScaffolder{}
    41	
    42	// apiScaffolder contains configuration for generating scaffolding for Go type
    43	// representing the API and controller that implements the behavior for the API.
    44	type apiScaffolder struct {
    45	        config    config.Config
    46	        resource  resource.Resource
    47	        image     string
    48	        command   string
    49	        port      string
    50	        runAsUser string
    51	
    52	        // fs is the filesystem that will be used by the scaffolder
    53	        fs machinery.Filesystem
    54	}
    55	
    56	// NewDeployImageScaffolder returns a new Scaffolder for declarative
    57	func NewDeployImageScaffolder(cfg config.Config, res resource.Resource, image,
    58	        command, port, runAsUser string,
    59	) plugins.Scaffolder {
    60	        return &apiScaffolder{
    61	                config:    cfg,
    62	                resource:  res,
    63	                image:     image,
    64	                command:   command,
    65	                port:      port,
    66	                runAsUser: runAsUser,
    67	        }
    68	}
    69	
    70	// InjectFS implements cmdutil.Scaffolder
    71	func (s *apiScaffolder) InjectFS(fs machinery.Filesystem) {
    72	        s.fs = fs
    73	}
    74	
    75	// Scaffold implements cmdutil.Scaffolder
    76	func (s *apiScaffolder) Scaffold() error {
    77	        log.Info("Writing scaffold for you to edit...")
    78	
    79	        if err := s.scaffoldCreateAPI(); err != nil {
    80	                return err
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        // Define the boilerplate file path
    84	        boilerplatePath := filepath.Join("hack", "boilerplate.go.txt")
    85	
    86	        // Load the boilerplate
    87	        boilerplate, err := afero.ReadFile(s.fs.FS, boilerplatePath)
    88	        if err != nil {
    89	                if errors.Is(err, afero.ErrFileNotFound) {
    90	                        log.Warn("unable to find boilerplate file. "+
    91	                                "This file is used to generate the license header in the project.\n"+
    92	                                "Note that controller-gen will also use this. Ensure that you "+
    93	                                "add the license file or configure your project accordingly",
    94	                                "file_path", boilerplatePath, "error", err)
    95	                        boilerplate = []byte("")
    96	                } else {
    97	                        return fmt.Errorf("error scaffolding API/controller: failed to load boilerplate: %w", err)
    98	                }
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        // Initialize the machinery.Scaffold that will write the files to disk
   102	        scaffold := machinery.NewScaffold(s.fs,
   103	                machinery.WithConfig(s.config),
   104	                machinery.WithBoilerplate(string(boilerplate)),
   105	                machinery.WithResource(&s.resource),
   106	        )
   107	
   108	        if err := scaffold.Execute(
   109	                &api.Types{Port: s.port},
   110	        ); err != nil {
   111	                return fmt.Errorf("error updating APIs: %w", err)
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        if err := scaffold.Execute(
   115	                &samples.CRDSample{Port: s.port},
   116	        ); err != nil {
   117	                return fmt.Errorf("error updating config/samples: %w", err)
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        controller := &controllers.Controller{
   121	                ControllerRuntimeVersion: golangv4scaffolds.ControllerRuntimeVersion,
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        if err := scaffold.Execute(
   125	                controller,

    55	// Scaffold uses templates to scaffold new files
    56	type Scaffold struct {
    57	        // fs allows to mock the file system for tests
    58	        fs afero.Fs
    59	
    60	        // permissions for new directories and files
    61	        dirPerm  os.FileMode
    62	        filePerm os.FileMode
    63	
    64	        // injector is used to provide several fields to the templates
    65	        injector injector
    66	}
    67	
    68	// ScaffoldOption allows to provide optional arguments to the Scaffold
    69	type ScaffoldOption func(*Scaffold)
    70	
    71	// NewScaffold returns a new Scaffold with the provided plugins
    72	func NewScaffold(fs Filesystem, options ...ScaffoldOption) *Scaffold {
    73	        s := &Scaffold{
    74	                fs:       fs.FS,
    75	                dirPerm:  DefaultDirectoryPermission,
    76	                filePerm: DefaultFilePermission,
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        for _, option := range options {
    80	                option(s)
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        return s
    84	}
    85	
    86	// WithDirectoryPermissions sets the permissions for new directories
    87	func WithDirectoryPermissions(dirPerm os.FileMode) ScaffoldOption {
    88	        return func(s *Scaffold) {
    89	                s.dirPerm = dirPerm
    90	        }
    91	}
    92	
    93	// WithFilePermissions sets the permissions for new files
    94	func WithFilePermissions(filePerm os.FileMode) ScaffoldOption {
    95	        return func(s *Scaffold) {
    96	                s.filePerm = filePerm
    97	        }
    98	}
    99	
   100	// WithConfig provides the project configuration to the Scaffold
   101	func WithConfig(cfg config.Config) ScaffoldOption {
   102	        return func(s *Scaffold) {
   103	                s.injector.config = cfg
   104	
   105	                if cfg != nil && cfg.GetRepository() != "" {
   106	                        imports.LocalPrefix = cfg.GetRepository()
   107	                }
   108	        }
   109	}
   110	
   111	// WithBoilerplate provides the boilerplate to the Scaffold
   112	func WithBoilerplate(boilerplate string) ScaffoldOption {
   113	        return func(s *Scaffold) {
   114	                s.injector.boilerplate = boilerplate
   115	        }
   116	}
   117	
   118	// WithResource provides the resource to the Scaffold
   119	func WithResource(res *resource.Resource) ScaffoldOption {
   120	        return func(s *Scaffold) {
   121	                s.injector.resource = res
   122	        }
   123	}

   125	// Execute writes to disk the provided files
   126	func (s *Scaffold) Execute(builders ...Builder) error {
   127	        // Initialize the files
   128	        files := make(map[string]*File, len(builders))
   129	
   130	        for _, builder := range builders {
   131	                // Inject common fields
   132	                s.injector.injectInto(builder)
   133	
   134	                // Validate file builders
   135	                if reqValBuilder, requiresValidation := builder.(RequiresValidation); requiresValidation {
   136	                        if err := reqValBuilder.Validate(); err != nil {
   137	                                return ValidateError{err}
   138	                        }
   139	                }
   140	
   141	                // Build models for Template builders
   142	                if t, isTemplate := builder.(Template); isTemplate {
   143	                        if err := s.buildFileModel(t, files); err != nil {
   144	                                return err
   145	                        }
   146	                }
   147	
   148	                // Build models for Inserter builders
   149	                if i, isInserter := builder.(Inserter); isInserter {
   150	                        if err := s.updateFileModel(i, files); err != nil {
   151	                                return err
   152	                        }
   153	                }
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        // Persist the files to disk
   157	        for _, f := range files {
   158	                if err := s.writeFile(f); err != nil {
   159	                        return err
   160	                }
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        return nil
   164	}
   165

   171	        }

   173	        path := t.GetPath()
   174	
   175	        // Handle already existing models
   176	        if _, found := models[path]; found {
   177	                switch t.GetIfExistsAction() {
   178	                case SkipFile:
   179	                        return nil
   180	                case Error:

    17	package machinery

    19	import (
    20	        "sigs.k8s.io/kubebuilder/v4/pkg/config"
    21	        "sigs.k8s.io/kubebuilder/v4/pkg/model/resource"
    22	)
    23	
    24	// injector is used to inject certain fields to file templates.
    25	type injector struct {
    26	        // config stores the project configuration.
    27	        config config.Config
    28	
    29	        // boilerplate is the copyright comment added at the top of scaffolded files.
    30	        boilerplate string
    31	
    32	        // resource contains the information of the API that is being scaffolded.
    33	        resource *resource.Resource
    34	}
    35	
    36	// injectInto injects fields from the universe into the builder
    37	func (i injector) injectInto(builder Builder) {
    38	        // Inject project configuration
    39	        if i.config != nil {
    40	                if builderWithDomain, hasDomain := builder.(HasDomain); hasDomain {
    41	                        builderWithDomain.InjectDomain(i.config.GetDomain())
    42	                }
    43	                if builderWithRepository, hasRepository := builder.(HasRepository); hasRepository {
    44	                        builderWithRepository.InjectRepository(i.config.GetRepository())
    45	                }
    46	                if builderWithProjectName, hasProjectName := builder.(HasProjectName); hasProjectName {
    47	                        builderWithProjectName.InjectProjectName(i.config.GetProjectName())

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/repro_year.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
current_year=$(date +%Y)

# init scaffolded boilerplate should keep the YEAR placeholder, not resolve to the current year.
grep -q 'f.Year = "YEAR"' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/hack/boilerplate.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: boilerplate template default does not scaffold YEAR placeholder'
  exit 1
}

# generated Makefile should define overridable YEAR and pass it to controller-gen.
grep -q 'YEAR ?= $(shell date +%Y)' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/makefile.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: Makefile template does not define YEAR ?= $(shell date +%Y)'
  exit 1
}
grep -q 'object:headerFile={{printf "%q" .BoilerplatePath}},year=$(YEAR)' pkg/plugins/golang/v4/scaffolds/internal/templates/makefile.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: Makefile template does not pass year=$(YEAR) to controller-gen with headerFile'
  exit 1
}

# boilerplate injected into subsequent scaffolded files should replace YEAR with current year.
grep -q 'strings.ReplaceAll(boilerplate, "YEAR", fmt.Sprintf("%d", time.Now().Year()))' pkg/machinery/mixins.go || {
  echo 'FAIL: boilerplate injection does not replace YEAR in boilerplate before scaffolding files'
  exit 1
}

echo 'PASS: YEAR placeholder support appears implemented'
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_year.sh
/tmp/repro_year.sh
